Task instruction sent to agent 
# Kubernetes API Server Admission Controller Chain

## Your Task

Find all Go source files in kubernetes/kubernetes that implement the API server admission controller pipeline: the admission.Interface registration, the generic admission chain execution, the mutating admission ordering, and the validating admission webhook call.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the platform domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/kubernetes--v1.32.0, sg-evals/client-go--v0.32.0, sg-evals/api--v0.32.0, sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd.


## Output Format

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:

```json
{
  "files": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go"}
  ],
  "symbols": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "SymbolName"}
  ],
  "chain": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "FunctionName"}
  ],
  "text": "Narrative explanation of your findings, citing repos and file paths."
}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

## Evaluation

Your answer will be scored on:
- **File recall and precision**: Did you find all relevant files?

    17	package admission
    18	
    19	import "context"
    20	
    21	// chainAdmissionHandler is an instance of admission.NamedHandler that performs admission control using
    22	// a chain of admission handlers
    23	type chainAdmissionHandler []Interface
    24	
    25	// NewChainHandler creates a new chain handler from an array of handlers. Used for testing.
    26	func NewChainHandler(handlers ...Interface) chainAdmissionHandler {
    27		return chainAdmissionHandler(handlers)
    28	}
    29	
    30	// Admit performs an admission control check using a chain of handlers, and returns immediately on first error
    31	func (admissionHandler chainAdmissionHandler) Admit(ctx context.Context, a Attributes, o ObjectInterfaces) error {
    32		for _, handler := range admissionHandler {
    33			if !handler.Handles(a.GetOperation()) {
    34				continue
    35			}
    36			if mutator, ok := handler.(MutationInterface); ok {
    37				err := mutator.Admit(ctx, a, o)
    38				if err != nil {
    39					return err
    40				}
    41			}
    42		}
    43		return nil
    44	}

    29	// Attributes is an interface used by AdmissionController to get information about a request
    30	// that is used to make an admission decision.
    31	type Attributes interface {
    32		// GetName returns the name of the object as presented in the request.  On a CREATE operation, the client
    33		// may omit name and rely on the server to generate the name.  If that is the case, this method will return
    34		// the empty string
    35		GetName() string
    36		// GetNamespace is the namespace associated with the request (if any)
    37		GetNamespace() string
    38		// GetResource is the name of the resource being requested.  This is not the kind.  For example: pods
    39		GetResource() schema.GroupVersionResource
    40		// GetSubresource is the name of the subresource being requested. 
... (truncated)

    31	// Factory is a function that returns an Interface for admission decisions.
    32	// The config parameter provides an io.Reader handler to the factory in
    33	// order to load specific configurations. If no configuration is provided
    34	// the parameter is nil.
    35	type Factory func(config io.Reader) (Interface, error)
    36	
    37	type Plugins struct {
    38		lock     sync.Mutex
    39		registry map[string]Factory
    40	}
    41	
    42	func NewPlugins() *Plugins {
    43		return &Plugins{}
    44	}
    45

    48		// PluginEnabledFn checks whether a plugin is enabled.  By default, if you ask about it, it's enabled.
    49		PluginEnabledFn = func(name string, config io.Reader) bool {
    50			return true
    51		}
    52	)

    21	// newReinvocationHandler creates a handler that wraps the provided admission chain and reinvokes it
    22	// if needed according to re-invocation policy of the webhooks.
    23	func newReinvocationHandler(admissionChain Interface) Interface {
    24		return &reinvoker{admissionChain}
    25	}
    26	
    27	type reinvoker struct {
    28		admissionChain Interface
    29	}
    30	
    31	// Admit performs an admission control check using the wrapped admission chain, reinvoking the
    32	// admission chain if needed according to the reinvocation policy.  Plugins are expected to check
    33	// the admission attributes' reinvocation context against their reinvocation policy to decide if
    34	// they should re-run, and to update the reinvocation context if they perform any mutations.
    35	func (r *reinvoker) Admit(ctx context.Context, a Attributes, o ObjectInterfaces) error {
    36		if mutator, ok := r.admissionChain.(MutationInterface); ok {
    37			err := mutator.Admit(ctx, a, o)
    38			if err != nil {
    39				return e

    33	// Register registers a plugin
    34	func Register(plugins *admission.Plugins) {
    35		plugins.Register(PluginName, func(configFile io.Reader) (admission.Interface, error) {
    36			plugin, err := NewMutatingWebhook(configFile)
    37			if err != nil {
    38				return nil, err
    39			}
    40	
    41			return plugin, nil
    42		})
    43	}

    40

    42	func (h *Handler) Handles(operation Operation) bool {
    43		return h.operations.Has(string(operation))
    44	}

    19	import (
    20		"os"

    23	
    24		"k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission"
    25	)
    26	
    27	// Config holds the configuration needed to for initialize the admission plugins
    28	type Config struct {
    29		CloudConfigFile string
    30	}
    31	
    32	// New sets up the plugins and admission start hooks needed for admission
    33	func (c *Config) New() ([]admission.PluginInitializer, error) {
    34		var cloudConfig []byte
    35		if c.CloudConfigFile != "" {
    36			var err error
    37			cloudConfig, err = os.ReadFile(c.CloudConfigFile)
    38			if err != nil {
    39				klog.Fatalf("Error reading from cloud configuration file %s: %#v", c.CloudConfigFile, err)
    40			}
    41		}
    42	
    43		return []admission.PluginInitializer{NewPluginInitializer(cloudConfig)}, nil
    44	}

    25	type webhookReinvokeContext struct {
    26		// lastWebhookOutput holds the result of the last webhook admission plugin call
    27		lastWebhookOutput runtime.Object
    28		// previouslyInvokedReinvocableWebhooks holds the set of webhooks that have been invoked and
    29		// should be reinvoked if a later mutation occurs
    30		previouslyInvokedReinvocableWebhooks sets.String
    31		// reinvokeWebhooks holds the set of webhooks that should be reinvoked
    32		reinvokeWebhooks sets.String
    33	}
    34	
    35	func (rc *webhookReinvokeContext) ShouldReinvokeWebhook(webhook string) bool {
    36		return rc.reinvokeWebhooks.Has(webhook)
    37	}
    38	
    39	func (rc *webhookReinvokeContext) IsOutputChangedSinceLastWebhookInvocation(object runtime.Object) bool {
    40		return !apiequality.Semantic.DeepEqual(rc.lastWebhookOutput, object)
    41	}

    59		}
    60	}

    63	// and provide the appropriate initialization data
    64	func (i pluginInitializer) Initialize(plugin admission.Interface) {
    65		// First tell the plugin about drained notification, so it can pass it to further initializations.

    68		}
    69	
    70		// Second tell the plugin about enabled features, so it can decide whether to start informers or not
    71		if wants, ok := plugin.(WantsFeatures); ok {
    72			wants.InspectFeatureGates(i.featureGates)
    73		}
    74	
    75		if wants, ok := plugin.(WantsExternalKubeClientSet); ok {
    76			wants.SetExternalKubeClientSet(i.externalClient)
    7

    17	package admission
    18	
    19	type Decorator interface {
    20		Decorate(handler Interface, name string) Interface
    21	}
    22	
    23	type DecoratorFunc func(handler Interface, name string) Interface
    24	
    25	func (d DecoratorFunc) Decorate(handler Interface, name string) Interface {
    26		return d(handler, name)
    27	}
    28	
    29	type Decorators []Decorator
    30	
    31	// Decorate applies the decorator in inside-out order, i.e. the first decorator in the slice is first applied to the given handler.
    32	func (d Decorators) Decorate(handler Interface, name string) Interface {
    33		result := handler
    34		for _, d := range d {
    35			result = d.Decorate(result, name)
    36		}
    37	
    38		return result
    39	}

    36	// of attribute into the audit event. Attributes passed to the Admit and
    37	// Validate function must be instance of privateAnnotationsGetter or

    40		if i == nil {

    42		}

    37	func makeAbs(path, base string) (string, error) {
    38		if filepath.IsAbs(path) {
    39			return path, nil
    40		}
    41		if len(base) == 0 || base == "." {
    42			cwd, err := os.Getwd()
    43			if err != nil {
    44				return "", err
    45			}
    46			base = cwd
    47		}
    48		return filepath.Join(base, path), nil
    49	}

## Kubernetes API Server Admission Controller Pipeline

The admission pipeline spans these key areas:

### Core Interfaces & Types
- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/interfaces.go` — Defines `Interface`, `MutationInterface`, `ValidationInterface`, `Attributes`, `PluginInitializer`, `ReinvocationContext`
- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugins.go` — `Plugins` registry with `Register()`, `NewFromPlugins()`, `InitPlugin()`
- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/chain.go` — `chainAdmissionHandler` iterating plugins in order
- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/reinvocation.go` — `reinvoker` implementing the re-invocation policy

### Plugin Registration
- `pkg/kubeapiserver/options/plugins.go` — `RegisterAllAdmissionPlugins()` + `AllOrderedPlugins` (canonical ordering)
- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/plugins.go` — generic `RegisterAllAdmissionPlugins()`

### Mutating Webhook
- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/plugin.go` — `Plugin` implementing `MutationInterface`
- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go` — sequential dispatch + patch application
- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/reinvocationcontext.go` — per-webhook reinvocation tracking

### Validating Webhook
- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/plugin.go` — `Plugin` implementing `ValidationInterface`
- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go` — concurrent parallel dispatch

### Shared Webhook Infrastructure
- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/webhook.go` — `W

across several packages in the kubernetes/kubernetes repository (primarily under staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/ which is also vendored from the apiserver module).\\n\\n## Core Admission Infrastructure\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/interfaces.go`** defines the foundational interfaces:\\n- `Interface`: base interface with `Handles(operation Operation) bool`\\n- `MutationInterface`: extends Interface with `Admit(ctx, a Attributes, o ObjectInterfaces) error` for mutating plugins\\n- `ValidationInterface`: extends Interface with `Validate(ctx, a Attributes, o ObjectInterfaces) error` for validating plugins\\n- `Attributes`: carries all request context (resource, operation, object, user, etc.)\\n- `PluginInitializer`: initializes plugins with shared resources\\n- `ReinvocationContext`: tracks reinvocation state for re-invocation policy\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/attributes.go`** implements `attributesRecord` (the concrete `Attributes`), created via `NewAttributesRecord()`.\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/handler.go`** provides `Handler`, the embeddable base struct for admission plugins implementing operation filtering and readiness.\\n\\n## Plugin Registration\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugins.go`** provides `Plugins` registry:\\n- `Register(name, Factory)`: registers a plugin factory\\n- `NewFromPlugins(pluginNames, configProvider, initializer, decorator)`: creates the full chain in order, returning a `reinvocationHandler` wrapping a `chainAdmissionHandler`\\n- `InitPlugin(name, config, initializer)`: instantiates and initializes one plugin\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/plugins.go`** - `RegisterAllAdmissionPlugins()` registers the generic built-in plugins (NamespaceLifecycle, MutatingAdmissionWebhook, ValidatingAdmissionWebhook, MutatingAdmissionPolicy, ValidatingAdmissionPolicy).\\n\\n**`pkg/kubeapiserver/options/plugins.go`** - kube-apiserver's `RegisterAllAdmissionPlugins()` registers all kube-specific plugins and defines `AllOrderedPlugins` which specifies the canonical ordering of all plugins (mutating before validating, with webhook plugins near the end).\\n\\n## Admission Chain Execution\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/chain.go`** implements `chainAdmissionHandler` (a `[]Interface`) which iterates through all plugins:\\n- `Admit()`: calls `MutationInterface.Admit()` for each plugin that handles the operation\\n- `Validate()`: calls `ValidationInterface.Validate()` for each plugin that handles the operation\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/reinvocation.go`** wraps the chain with `reinvoker`:\\n- `Admit()`: runs the chain once, then if `ShouldReinvoke()` is true, runs it a second time (re-invocation policy)\\n- This is how mutating admission plugins get a second chance when a later plugin mutates the object\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/audit.go`** - `WithAudit()` wraps the chain to log audit annotations after Admit/Validate calls.\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/decorator.go`** - `Decorators` applies a list of `Decorator`s around each plugin (e.g., metrics instrumentation).\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/metrics/metrics.go`** - `WithControllerMetrics` decorates each named plugin, `WithStepMetrics` decorates the entire chain.\\n\\n## Mutating Admission Ordering\\n\\nThe `AllOrderedPlugins` list in `pkg/kubeapiserver/options/plugins.go` defines that all mutating plugins (in-tree controllers + MutatingAdmissionPolicy + MutatingAdmissionWebhook) run before all validating plugins (ValidatingAdmissionPolicy + ValidatingAdmissionWebhook). The `chainAdmissionHandler` respects this by calling `Admit()` only on `MutationInterface` implementors and `Validate()` only on `ValidationInterface` implementors in order. The `reinvoker` enables the re-invocation policy where webhooks with `IfNeeded` policy can be called again if subsequent plugins mutate the object.\\n\\n## Mutating Webhook Admission\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/plugin.go`**: `Plugin` implements `admission.MutationInterface`. `Register()` registers it as `MutatingAdmissionWebhook`. `Admit()` calls `a.Webhook.Dispatch()`.\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/webhook.go`**: `Webhook` base struct shared by mutating and validating webhook plugins. `Dispatch()` checks if ready, fetches webhooks from `hookSource`, then calls `dispatcher.Dispatch()`. `ShouldCallHook()` checks namespace selector, object selector, and rules matching.\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go`**: `mutatingDispatcher.Dispatch()` iterates webhooks in order (sequentially, not in parallel), checks re-invocation context, calls `callAttrMutatingHook()` which makes the HTTP call to the webhook, applies the returned JSON patch to the object, and marks the context for reinvocation if mutations occurred.\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/reinvocationcontext.go`**: `webhookReinvokeContext` tracks which webhooks have been invoked and should be re-invoked.\\n\\n## Validating Webhook Admission\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/plugin.go`**: `Plugin` implements `admission.ValidationInterface`. `Register()` registers it as `ValidatingAdmissionWebhook`. `Validate()` calls `a.Webhook.Dispatch()`.\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go`**: `validatingDispatcher.Dispatch()` collects relevant hooks, then calls them concurrently (using goroutines and `sync.WaitGroup`). `callHook()` makes the HTTP call and checks the response.\\n\\n## Webhook Support Infrastructure\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/accessors.go`**: `WebhookAccessor` interface provides uniform access to both mutating and validating webhook configurations.\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/request/admissionreview.go`**: `CreateAdmissionObjects()` builds the AdmissionReview request; `VerifyAdmissionResponse()` validates the webhook response.\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/matchconditions/matcher.go`**: CEL-based match condition evaluation for webhooks.\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/predicates/`**: namespace selector, object selector, and rule matching predicates used by `ShouldCallHook()`.\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/`**: `mutating_webhook_manager.go` and `validating_webhook_manager.go` watch the API server for `MutatingWebhookConfiguration` and `ValidatingWebhookConfiguration` objects and maintain the live webhook list.\\n\\n## Admission Policy (CEL-based)\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/policy/mutating/plugin.go`** and **`validating/plugin.go`**: CEL-based admission policies (MutatingAdmissionPolicy / ValidatingAdmissionPolicy) that compile and evaluate CEL expressions.\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/policy/generic/plugin.go`**: Generic policy plugin base with `Dispatch()` method shared by both policy types.\\n\\n## Plugin Initialization\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/initializer/initializer.go`**: Generic `pluginInitializer` providing ClientSet, InformerFactory, Authorizer, FeatureGates, etc. to plugins that declare corresponding `Wants*` interfaces.\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/initializer/initializer.go`**: Webhook-specific initializer providing `ServiceResolver` and `AuthenticationInfoResolverWrapper`.\\n\\n**`pkg/kubeapiserver/admission/initializer.go`**: Kube-specific initializer providing cloud configuration.\\n\\n## Chain Assembly\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/options/admission.go`**: `AdmissionOptions.ApplyTo()` orchestrates chain assembly: reads plugin config, creates generic+kube initializers, calls `Plugins.NewFromPlugins()` to build the chain, wraps with `WithStepMetrics()`, and assigns to `c.AdmissionControl`.\\n\\n## Request Invocation\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/handlers/create.go`**: `createHandler()` calls `mutatingAdmission.Admit()` before storage, and passes `AdmissionToValidateObjectFunc()` (which calls `validatingAdmission.Validate()`) to the storage layer.\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/registry/rest/create.go`**: `AdmissionToValidateObjectFunc()` converts the `ValidationInterface` to a `ValidateObjectFunc` called by the storage layer at write time.\\n\\nSimilar patterns apply in `update.go`, `patch.go`, and `rest.go` (for CONNECT operations).\"\n}\nENDJSON\necho \"Done\"",

  "text": "The Kubernetes API server admission controller pipeline is implemented across several packages in the kubernetes/kubernetes repository (primarily under staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/ which is also vendored from the apiserver module).\n\n## Core Admission Infrastructure\n\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/interfaces.go`** defines the foundational interfaces:\n- `Interface`: base interface with `Handles(operation Operation) bool`\n- `MutationInterface`: extends Interface with `Admit(ctx, a Attributes, o ObjectInterfaces) error` for mutating plugins\n- `ValidationInterface`: extends Interface with `Validate(ctx, a Attributes, o ObjectInterfaces) error` for validating plugins\n- `Attributes`: carries all request context (resource, operation, object, user, etc.)\n- `PluginInitializer`: initializes plugins with shared resources\n- `ReinvocationContext`: tracks reinvocation state for re-invocation policy\n\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/attributes.go`** implements `attributesRecord` (the concrete `Attributes`), created via `NewAttributesRecord()`.\n\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/handler.go`** provides `Handler`, the embeddable base struct for admission plugins implementing operation filtering and readiness.\n\n## Plugin Registration\n\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugins.go`** provides `Plugins` registry:\n- `Register(name, Factory)`: registers a plugin factory\n- `NewFromPlugins(pluginNames, configProvider, initializer, decorator)`: creates the full chain in order, returning a `reinvocationHandler` wrapping a `chainAdmissionHandler`\n- `InitPlugin(name, config, initializer)`: instantiates and initializes one plugin\n\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/plugins.go`** - `RegisterAllAdmissionPlugins()` registers the generic built-in plugins (NamespaceLifecycle, MutatingAdmissionWebhook, ValidatingAdmissionWebhook, MutatingAdmissionPolicy, ValidatingAdmissionPolicy).\n\n**`pkg/kubeapiserver/options/plugins.go`** - kube-apiserver's `RegisterAllAdmissionPlugins()` registers all kube-specific plugins and defines `AllOrderedPlugins` which specifies the canonical ordering of all plugins (mutating before validating, with webhook plugins near the end).\n\n## Admission Chain Execution\n\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/chain.go`** implements `chainAdmissionHandler` (a `[]Interface`) which iterates through all plugins:\n- `Admit()`: calls `MutationInterface.Admit()` for each plugin that handles the operation\n- `Validate()`: calls `ValidationInterface.Validate()` for each plugin that handles the operation\n\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/reinvocation.go`** wraps the chain with `reinvoker`:\n- `Admit()`: runs the chain once, then if `ShouldReinvoke()` is true, runs it a second time (re-invocation policy)\n- This is how mutating admission plugins get a second chance when a later plugin mutates the object\n\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/audit.go`** - `WithAudit()` wraps the chain to log audit annotations after Admit/Validate calls.\n\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/decorator.go`** - `Decorators` applies a list of `Decorator`s around each plugin (e.g., metrics instrumentation).\n\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/metrics/metrics.go`** - `WithControllerMetrics` decorates each named plugin, `WithStepMetrics` decorates the entire chain.\n\n## Mutating Admission Ordering\n\nThe `AllOrderedPlugins` list in `pkg/kubeapiserver/options/plugins.go` defines that all mutating plugins (in-tree controllers + MutatingAdmissionPolicy + MutatingAdmissionWebhook) run before all validating plugins (ValidatingAdmissionPolicy + ValidatingAdmissionWebhook). The `chainAdmissionHandler` respects this by calling `Admit()` only on `MutationInterface` implementors and `Validate()` only on `ValidationInterface` implementors in order. The `reinvoker` enables the re-invocation policy where webhooks with `IfNeeded` policy can be called again if subsequent plugins mutate the object.\n\n## Mutating Webhook Admission\n\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/plugin.go`**: `Plugin` implements `admission.MutationInterface`. `Register()` registers it as `MutatingAdmissionWebhook`. `Admit()` calls `a.Webhook.Dispatch()`.\n\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/webhook.go`**: `Webhook` base struct shared by mutating and validating webhook plugins. `Dispatch()` checks if ready, fetches webhooks from `hookSource`, then calls `dispatcher.Dispatch()`. `ShouldCallHook()` checks namespace selector, object selector, and rules matching.\n\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go`**: `mutatingDispatcher.Dispatch()` iterates webhooks in order (sequentially, not in parallel), checks re-invocation context, calls `callAttrMutatingHook()` which makes the HTTP call to the webhook, applies the returned JSON patch to the object, and marks the context for reinvocation if mutations occurred.\n\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/reinvocationcontext.go`**: `webhookReinvokeContext` tracks which webhooks have been invoked and should be re-invoked.\n\n## Validating Webhook Admission\n\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/plugin.go`**: `Plugin` implements `admission.ValidationInterface`. `Register()` registers it as `ValidatingAdmissionWebhook`. `Validate()` calls `a.Webhook.Dispatch()`.\n\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go`**: `validatingDispatcher.Dispatch()` collects relevant hooks, then calls them concurrently (using goroutines and `sync.WaitGroup`). `callHook()` makes the HTTP call and checks the response.\n\n## Webhook Support Infrastructure\n\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/accessors.go`**: `WebhookAccessor` interface provides uniform access to both mutating and validating webhook configurations.\n\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/request/admissionreview.go`**: `CreateAdmissionObjects()` builds the AdmissionReview request; `VerifyAdmissionResponse()` validates the webhook response.\n\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/matchconditions/matcher.go`**: CEL-based match condition evaluation for webhooks.\n\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/predicates/`**: namespace selector, object selector, and rule matching predicates used by `ShouldCallHook()`.\n\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/`**: `mutating_webhook_manager.go` and `validating_webhook_manager.go` watch the API server for `MutatingWebhookConfiguration` and `ValidatingWebhookConfiguration` objects and maintain the live webhook list.\n\n## Admission Policy (CEL-based)\n\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/policy/mutating/plugin.go`** and **`validating/plugin.go`**: CEL-based admission policies (MutatingAdmissionPolicy / ValidatingAdmissionPolicy) that compile and evaluate CEL expressions.\n\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/policy/generic/plugin.go`**: Generic policy plugin base with `Dispatch()` method shared by both policy types.\n\n## Plugin Initialization\n\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/initializer/initializer.go`**: Generic `pluginInitializer` providing ClientSet, InformerFactory, Authorizer, FeatureGates, etc. to plugins that declare corresponding `Wants*` interfaces.\n\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/initializer/initializer.go`**: Webhook-specific initializer providing `ServiceResolver` and `AuthenticationInfoResolverWrapper`.\n\n**`pkg/kubeapiserver/admission/initializer.go`**: Kube-specific initializer providing cloud configuration.\n\n## Chain Assembly\n\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/options/admission.go`**: `AdmissionOptions.ApplyTo()` orchestrates chain assembly: reads plugin config, creates generic+kube initializers, calls `Plugins.NewFromPlugins()` to build the chain, wraps with `WithStepMetrics()`, and assigns to `c.AdmissionControl`.\n\n## Request Invocation\n\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/handlers/create.go`**: `createHandler()` calls `mutatingAdmission.Admit()` before storage, and passes `AdmissionToValidateObjectFunc()` (which calls `validatingAdmission.Validate()`) to the storage layer.\n\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/registry/rest/create.go`**: `AdmissionToValidateObjectFunc()` converts the `ValidationInterface` to a `ValidateObjectFunc` called by the storage layer at write time.\n\nSimilar patterns apply in `update.go`, `patch.go`, and `rest.go` (for CONNECT operations)."
}
ENDJSON
